< Text>
A very small, hole in the wall place with a big menu! Bravo to the chef, who was willing to accommodate our request for low sodium and no MSG. The food was almost as good as  the Chinese in the SG Valley. Why almost? This place does not specialize in any particular item, like juicy pork dumplings or vegetarian, etc. However, for any general Chinese, like Orange Chicken, Beef w Broccoli, Saut√©ed Spinach, Moo Shu Chicken, dumplings, or chow mien, it's absolutely decent. The price is competitive for the Westside. The only thing I found a bit "disturbing" was the loud voices of the workers speaking Chinese while on the phone or talking to each other. But that brought me and my family back to Chinatown, without going all the way there, so it was fun in a way... Here is my advice: Go here for good Chinese, not for the romantic ambience.<//Text>

<Time>1468259222172< /Time>< review>
I can't rate this as a 5 because Monterey Park and Alhambra are reasonably close.

This is among the best in the Westside. And the prices are absolutely great for a Westside restaurant!

I consider this place a "go-to" when I'm craving Chinese food but don't want to go all the way to Monterey Park.

Oh, and service is pretty lame. Need to get their attention if you want to be served. But that's typical for a Cantonese restaurant, so I'm not going to fault them on this.

They also have online ordering! Nice! Very convenient indeed. And free delivery!

Legit :-)</review>

< text>
Service was prompt. Bartender had limited skills. The house salad was divine. My entree was enjoyable, but for some unknown reason, was covered in fresh vegetable straw. It buried the meal. It was so overwhelming that it moved it to my bread plate which could not carry it's load. What was it's purpose?  Filler?  The story was what was under the hay... Tender shrimp and scallops. Amen.

Reheated steamed rolls quickly turned into rocks.  Come on guys, you can do better. You are so close to having your act together.

Others at the table had ordered steak. This was not a steakhouse, and that should have been your warning not to order it.  Both steaks were flavorless.

I'll be back, because I'm not giving up on you. Please try harder...< /text>

<Pictures>None</Pictures><text>We recently dined at the reopened restaurant. It was a dispiriting experience, in terms of atmosphere, service, and food. Although the interior retains its cool, dimly-lit elegance, the table settings were missing: no chargers, no plates, no flatware, no salt and pepper shakers, no flowers - just a barren table top. Service was certainly not spot-on. Even though the restaurant was at half capacity, and there seemed to be plenty of servers around,  service was slow and impersonal. The hostess who seated us without any greeting wasn't welcoming or even attractively dressed. (No Ginger there.) Once at our table, we had to ask for place settings and bread, drinks took a while to arrive, the wine service perfunctory, and there was no follow-up after the courses were presented. As for the food, the menu hasn't been changed for years, and one gets the impression that it is all prepared ahead of time, especially the sides, with little imagination or interest from the kitchen.

A notice on the front door indicates that the restaurant has new owners. Will they return this very special place to its former "glory" or continue its decline?</text>< user_id>

<Text>Very good American food restaurant which been around for a long time. Famous for its liver dish. I never tried it. But wild mushrooms ravioli, atlantic salmon fillet /actually baked with dill and horseradish and yammy mushed potatoes/, and seared ahi tuna were pretty good. Comes with choice of soup or salad. They have special fix dinner in the summer. Nice elegant but relaxed ambience. Restaurant stays on its own without surrounding businesses so easy parking. Considered the best nice casual restaurant by "old money" so to speak, for many decades. Not much of old money left - went to Attorneys and now aging children fighting over it.< /Text>< response>

This is a local favorite, less well-known by tourists, but the good times roll on both during High Season, & all year.  The food isn't the very best in the Coachella Valley, but it IS consistently very, very good.

<username>Gilbert Melby< /username><Time>1403710877413< /Time>< Rate>
2</Rate>
< review>
We have been to Shame on the Moon probably 4-5 times in the last several years, and based on the experience before the one we had recently, thought we were in for another great meal and service that you would expect at a restaurant like this.  Unfortunately, the evening started out badly when they crammed (literally!) 10 of us into the corner of the porch on very hard chairs.  I could not sit without crossing my legs at the ankles.  This table should have held at most 8 people!  Then the filet I ordered came with a blue cheese coating that overpowered the steak and with a corn something or other that was inedible.  In checking with another diner at our table, their meal was likewise unappealing.  I don't know what happened with the seating arrangement, or if they commonly sit that many people in that corner, but I don't think so.  A visit to a chiropractor is almost necessary after sitting in that uncomfortable position for 2 hours.  As for the filet, the meat itself was fine...the blue cheese covering it....NOT!  And get rid of those corn fritters or whatever they're called. We may be back or not and see if anything has improved.  There are too many really good restaurants in the valley to choose from when you have a negative experience like this.< /review>

< text>
I recently had a horrible experience here first of the restaurant was hot the fans are no longer working and it seems as if the ac isn't either. We decided to order a bottle of wine and it was served at the hot restaurant tempture. This place totes it's self as a high end restaurant and I would expect a 30+ bottle of wine to be chilled properly and served at 68 degrees not 80.

After that the salad that was served was wilted probably suffering under the hot tempture like the rest of us. The soup was unsalted and the beans were undercooked. The salmon we got was beyond over cooked and so was the filet mignon which had cheese melted on it. The ahi tuna that I got was raw and how I ordered iy but some how dry probably frozen and cooked in a pan that was to hot.  The flank steak was just bad, over cooked and smothered in an awful sauce.

I complained about the issues and was comped the wine after the manager argued with me saying I was being unreasonable. I would not go again and if you are any kind of foodie or have ever been to a decent restaurant in you life you will hate the food and the price that you will pay for what you are getting.<//text>

<review>I had to write a long review, I felt it was only fair to do so. I don't take the time to do this, but I had to give credit where credit is due. I purchased a 2016 WRX over a year and a half ago but put 48,000 miles on it during that period due to long commutes to the Bay Area.

My release bearing (Throw-Out Bearing) was making a lot of noise, and my steering box was also making a lot of noise. After my car was diagnosed by Modesto Subaru, it was concluded that it needed a new clutch throw-out bearing, and a new steering rack. The only problem with that was; my warranty had expired at 36,000 and only the engine and transmission were covered up to 60K miles.

I spoke with Nelson Peterson, the sales manager that had taken good care of me when I purchased the car. He said he would try his best to have the dealer cover the expensive repairs at not cost. Nelson spoke with Carl Hansen, the service manager and Carl told me that he wouldn't promise anything, but he would try to cover it at no cost.

A week went by and I received a call from Carl telling me that he had ordered my parts, and the dealer would cover the repair costs at no charge.

I was so happy to hear this and felt that both Nelson and Carl truly treated me like a valued customer, and really cared about long-term relationship not just one time sale.

The repairs were made, I was given a brand-new loaner car (Forester) and didn't pay a cent for all this. Daniel Di Dio (Dan) was also very nice to me and kept me posted throughout the process.

I can't say enough about this dealership and the staff, I have never ever experienced this level of great customer service. The repairs were over $2K and didn't pay a cent. They could've easily told me that the warranty was expired and they couldn't do anything about it, instead they earned a loyal customer for life.

This is the most honest and caring dealership I have ever dealt with and I have been leasing and buying cars since 1999 and have dealt with many dealership in the Modesto area. Modesto Subaru is where I will go for my next car.

Thank you Nelson and Carl and everyone that made this possible. I love you guys and love my WRX.<//review>< Pictures>
